Resources

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept?page_size&page

Methods

GET

Gets the paged list of all IfdConcepts. Will return the list with up to 100 elements, or lower if specified. If page is specified it will return the list from the page You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_ADMINISTRATOR</a> access to use this method. Undocumented API

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

page_size

page

the cursor returned from the previous page in it's header parameter "Next-Page"

available response representations:

  • application/xml
  • application/json

POST

Creates a new concept in bsDD Names and descriptions must be existing or be added before a new concept can be added. As a minimum a name in international English and another language must be provided. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdBase)
  • application/json

Methods

POST

Creates a new concept in bsDD Names and descriptions must be existing or be added before a new concept can be added. As a minimum a name in international English and another language must be provided. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdBase)

//json/IfdConcept

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/list?guids

Methods

GET

Gets a list of concepts from a list of global unique identifiers (GUIDs). If GUIDs for concepts that has been merged is provided then the new merged concepts is returned different GUIDs. No error message is given. Software should therefore test the provided GUID against the returned GUID to check if the original concept has been merged. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_READ_AND_COMMENT</a> access to use this method.

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

guids

a comma separated list of the global unique identifier for the concept

available response representations:

  • application/xml
  • application/json

//xml/IfdConcept/list?guids

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/search

Methods

POST

This function uses POST instead of GET <br> Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. Will return a paged list with up to 100 elements, or lower if specified. If page is specified it will return the list from the page You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

//xml/IfdConcept/search

Methods

POST

This function uses POST instead of GET <br> Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. Will return a paged list with up to 100 elements, or lower if specified. If page is specified it will return the list from the page You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)

//json/IfdConcept/search

Methods

POST

This function uses POST instead of GET <br> Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. Will return a paged list with up to 100 elements, or lower if specified. If page is specified it will return the list from the page You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/json

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/searchForDuplicates

Methods

POST

This method tries to list candidates that could be possible duplicates of concepts for which the list of names given, belongs. There is always a chance that a concept not returned here might still be a duplicate. The list returned here is not necessarily exhaustive. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/{guid}

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

guid

the 32 character global unique identifier for the concept

Methods

GET

Gets one concept from its global unique identifier (GUID). If a GUID for a concept that has been merged is provided then the new merged concept is returned with a different GUID. No error message is given. Software should therefore test the provided GUID against the returned GUID to check if the original concept has been merged. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

DELETE

Removes the concept from the buildingSMART Data Dictionary. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_ADMINISTRATOR</a> access to use this method. Undocumented API

Methods

GET

Gets the <a href="el_objects_IfdName.html">IfdName</a> object with the given GUID You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdName)
  • application/json

PUT

Update a name with the given GUID. All parameters must be provided. If any parameter should be unchanged, just provide the original value in the parameter. If this name is used by several concepts, this change will be reflected for all those concepts. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method.

DELETE

Removes the name with the given GUID from bSDD. Note, this will remove the name completely from bSDD, so no concept will no longer use this name. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method.

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/preferred/list?guids

Methods

GET

Gets a list of concepts from a list of global unique identifiers (GUIDs), with only preferred names/descriptions/illustrations attached. Names/descriptions/illustrations attached to the concepts that is not preferred by the organization of the calling user will not be returned. If GUIDs for concepts that has been merged is provided then the new merged concepts is returned different GUIDs. No error message is given. Software should therefore test the provided GUID against the returned GUID to check if the original concept has been merged. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_READ_AND_COMMENT</a> access to use this method.

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

guids

a comma separated list of the global unique identifier for the concept

available response representations:

  • application/xml
  • application/json

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/search/{searchString}?page_size&page&cache

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

searchString

the search string on UTF-8 format

Methods

GET

Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. Will return a paged list with up to 100 elements, or lower if specified. If page is specified it will return the list from the page You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

page_size

page

the cursor returned from the previous page in it's header parameter "Next-Page"

cache

you will receive cached data unless value is "false"

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

//json/IfdConcept/search/{searchString}?page_size&page&cache

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

searchString

the search string on UTF-8 format

Methods

GET

Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. Will return a paged list with up to 100 elements, or lower if specified. If page is specified it will return the list from the page You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

page_size

page

the cursor returned from the previous page in it's header parameter "Next-Page"

cache

you will receive cached data unless value is "false"

available response representations:

  • application/json

POST

Copies one context to another, so that all relations with the given context will also be part of the copyToContextGuid given. Useful to start out with content of some chosen quality and type. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method, AND you need to have access to context to copy from and be owner of context to copy to.

parametervaluedescription

the search string in UTF-8 format

Methods

GET

Search for a name in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as a wildcard character. You can search using * in the end of the search string not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names and lexemes for the given string. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

page_size

page

the cursor returned from the previous page in it's header parameter "Next-Page"

available response representations:

  • application/xml
  • application/json

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

sandboxGuid

the GUID of the sandbox to which the sandbox concept belongs to

guid

the GUID of the sandbox concept to request

Methods

GET

Gets the sandbox concept with the given GUID. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_READ_ONLY</a> access to use this method, AND you need to have proper access rights to the sandbox it belongs to.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdSandboxConcept)
  • application/json

DELETE

Removes the the sandbox concept. This also removes all data attached to this concept, e.g names, that are not in use by other concepts! You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method, AND you need proper access to the sandbox where the sandbox concept belongs.

//../api/4.0/IfdUser/search/{searchString}

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

searchString

the search string on UTF-8 format

Methods

GET

Search for an user in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wild card characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search user names for the search string. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">ADMINISTRATOR</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/search/filter/language

Methods

POST

This function uses POST instead of GET. <br> Search with language filter. <br> Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character, and with the additional filtering on language. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

//../api/4.0/IfdName/{guid}/forConcept/{conceptGuid}

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

guid

the GUID of the name to update

conceptGuid

the GUID of the concept for which the update should apply

Methods

PUT

Update a name only for a given concept. All parameters must be provided. If any parameter should be unchanged, just provide the original value in the parameter. If this name is used by several concepts, a new name is created for this concept and the old name kept for all the other concepts. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method.

If this name is used by several concepts, a new name is created for this concept and the old name kept for all the other concepts. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method.

//../api/4.0/IfdName/{guid}/forConceptGetNameGuid/{conceptGuid}

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

guid

the GUID of the name to update

conceptGuid

the GUID of the concept for which the update should apply

Methods

PUT

Update a name only for a given concept. All parameters must be provided. If any parameter should be unchanged, just provide the original value in the parameter. If this name is used by several concepts, a new name is created for this concept and the old name kept for all the other concepts. This method returns the guid of updated name as IfdBase object. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdBase)
  • application/json

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/search/filter/language/type

Methods

POST

This function uses POST instead of GET. <br> Search with language and type filter. <br> Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character, and with the additional filtering on both language and concept type. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

//xml/IfdConcept/search/filter/language/type

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/searchForDuplicates/filter/type/{conceptType}

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

conceptType

the <a href="objects_IfdConceptTypeEnum.html">type</a> of concept to filter on

Methods

POST

This method tries to list candidates that could be possible duplicates of concepts for which the list of names given, belongs. There is always a chance that a concept not returned here might still be a duplicate. The list returned here is not necessarily exhaustive. The list is filtered on the given concept type. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

Search for concepts in the sandboxes you have access to with concept type and language filter (this method uses POST instead of GET). You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_READ_ONLY</a> access to use this method.

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdSandboxConcept)

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/search/filter/language/{languageGuid}/{searchString}?page_size&page&cache

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

searchString

the search string on UTF-8 format

languageGuid

the language GUID for the language used as filter

Methods

GET

* Search with language filter. <br> Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character, and with the additional filtering on language. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. Will return a paged list with up to 100 elements, or lower if specified. If page is specified it will return the list from the page You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

page_size

page

the cursor returned from the previous page in it's header parameter "Next-Page"

cache

you will receive cached data unless value is "false"

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

//../api/4.0/IfdConcept/search/filter/language/{languageGuid}/type/{conceptType}/{searchString}?page_size&page&cache

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

searchString

the search string on UTF-8 format

languageGuid

the language GUID for the language used as filter

conceptType

filter by one of the following concept types <a href="objects_ifdConceptTypeEnum.html">ifdConceptTypeEnum</a>

Methods

GET

Search with language and type filter. <br> Search for a concept in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character, and with the additional filtering on both language and concept type. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as wildcard characters. You can search using * in the end of a sentence not inside or in the beginning. The API will search full-names, short-names for the given string. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

page_size

page

the cursor returned from the previous page in it's header parameter "Next-Page"

cache

you will receive cached data unless value is "false"

available response representations:

  • application/xml (objects:IfdConcept)
  • application/json

guid

the GUID of the concept from which you want to remove the parent

parentGuid

the GUID of the parent to be removed

relationshipType

the <a href="objects_IfdRelationshipTypeEnum.html">relationship type</a>

contextGuids

the GUIDs of the contexts of this relationship

Methods

DELETE

Removes the contexts from the relationship between the concept and the parent. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">IFD_EDITOR</a> access to use this method.

//../api/4.0/IfdName/search/filter/language/{languageGuid}/nametype/{nameType}/{searchString}?page_size&page

resource-wide template parameters
parametervaluedescription

searchString

the search string in UTF-8 format

nameType

the <a href="objects_IfdNameTypeEnum.html">type</a> of name to filter on

languageGuid

the GUID of the language to filter on

Methods

GET

Do a filtered search for a name in bSDD by a search string consisting with a minimum length of 1 character. The search string must be provided in UTF-8 format and only * is allowed as a wildcard character. You can search using * in the end of the search string not inside or in the beginning. You need minimum <a href="objects_IfdUserRoleTypeEnum.html">PUBLIC</a> access to use this method.

request query parameters
parametervaluedescription

page_size

page

the cursor returned from the previous page in it's header parameter "Next-Page"

available response representations:

  • application/xml
  • application/json
